\"\"\"Thread-safe streaming of job results to CSV.\"\"\"\n    with lock:\n        for job in jobs:\n            csv_writer.writerow({\n                \"zip_code\": zip_code,\n                         "import threading\nimport queue\nimport requests\nimport time\nimport random\nimport csv\nimport os\nfrom openpyxl import load_workbook\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# ------------------- CONFIGURATION -------------------\nINDEED_SEARCH_URL = \"https://www.indeed.com/jobs\"\nHEADERS = {\n    \"User-Agent\": \"Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) \"\n                  \"AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) \"\n                  \"Chrome/114.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\"\n}\nPROXY_LIST_FILE = \"proxies.txt\"  # Each line: http://user:pass@ip:port or http://ip:port\nZIP_XLSX_FILE = \"zipcodes.xlsx\"  # Input .xlsx file with ZIP codes in first column\nOUTPUT_CSV_FILE = \"indeed_jobs.csv\"\nNUM_THREADS = 20  # Adjust based on system/network\n\n# ------------------- PROXY ROTATION -------------------\ndef load_proxies(proxy_file):\n    proxies = []\n    if os.path.exists(proxy_file):\n        with open(proxy_file, \"r\") as f:\n            for line in f:\n                proxy = line.strip()\n                if proxy:\n                    proxies.append(proxy)\n    return proxies\n\nclass ProxyRotator:\n    def __init__(self, proxies):\n        self.proxies = proxies\n        self.lock = threading.Lock()\n        self.idx = 0\n\n    def get_proxy(self):\n        with self.lock:\n            if not self.proxies:\n                return None\n            proxy = self.proxies[self.idx]\n            self.idx = (self.idx + 1) % len(self.proxies)\n            return {\n                \"http\": proxy,\n                \"https\": proxy\n            }\n\n# ------------------- ZIP CODE LOADER -------------------\ndef load_zipcodes(xlsx_file):\n    wb = load_workbook(xlsx_file)\n    ws = wb.active\n    zipcodes = []\n    for row in ws.iter_rows(min_row=2, values_only=True):  # Assuming header in row 1\n        zip_code = str(row[0]).strip()\n        if zip_code and zip_code.isdigit():\n            zipcodes.append(zip_code)\n    return zipcodes\n\n# ------------------- SCRAPER LOGIC -------------------\ndef scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator):\n    \"\"\"\n    Scrapes Indeed jobs for a given ZIP code.\n    Returns a list of dicts with job details.\n    \"\"\"\n    jobs = []\n    params = {\n        \"l\": zip_code,\n        \"radius\": \"25\",  # 25 miles radius\n        \"limit\": \"50\",   # max results per page\n        \"start\": \"0\"\n    }\n    max_pages = 3  # Limit pages per ZIP to avoid excessive requests\n    for page in range(max_pages):\n        params[\"start\"] = str(page * 50)\n        proxy = proxy_rotator.get_proxy()\n        try:\n            response = requests.get(\n                INDEED_SEARCH_URL,\n                params=params,\n                headers=HEADERS,\n                proxies=proxy,\n                timeout=15\n            )\n            if response.status_code != 200:\n                continue\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, \"html.parser\")\n            job_cards = soup.find_all(\"div\", class_=\"job_seen_beacon\")\n            if not job_cards:\n                break  # No jobs found, stop paging\n\n            for card in job_cards:\n                title_tag = card.find(\"h2\", class_=\"jobTitle\")\n                title = title_tag.text.strip() if title_tag else \"\"\n                company_tag = card.find(\"span\", class_=\"companyName\")\n                company = company_tag.text.strip() if company_tag else \"\"\n                location_tag = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"companyLocation\")\n                location = location_tag.text.strip() if location_tag else \"\"\n                summary_tag = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"job-snippet\")\n                summary = summary_tag.text.strip().replace(\"\\n\", \" \") if summary_tag else \"\"\n                job_url_tag = card.find(\"a\", href=True)\n                job_url = (\"https://www.indeed.com\" + job_url_tag['href']) if job_url_tag else \"\"\n                jobs.append({\n                    \"zip_code\": zip_code,\n                    \"title\": title,\n                    \"company\": company,\n                    \"location\": location,\n                    \"summary\": summary,\n                    \"job_url\": job_url\n                })\n            time.sleep(random.uniform(0.5, 1.5))  # polite delay\n        except Exception as e:\n            # Could log error for zip_code\n            time.sleep(1)\n            continue\n    return jobs\n\n# ------------------- MULTITHREADING -------------------\ndef worker(zip_queue, proxy_rotator, result_queue):\n    while True:\n        try:\n            zip_code = zip_queue.get(timeout=3)\n        except queue.Empty:\n            break\n        jobs = scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator)\n        for job in jobs:\n            result_queue.put(job)\n        zip_queue.task_done()\n\n# ------------------- CSV STREAM WRITER -------------------\ndef csv_writer(result_queue, output_file, stop_event):\n    fieldnames = [\"zip_code\", \"title\", \"company\", \"location\", \"summary\", \"job_url\"]\n    with open(output_file, \"w\", newline='', encoding=\"utf-8\") as csvfile:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        while not stop_event.is_set() or not result_queue.empty():\n            try:\n                job = result_queue.get(timeout=2)\n                writer.writerow(job)\n                result_queue.task_done()\n            except queue.Empty:\n                continue\n\n# ------------------- MAIN -------------------\ndef main():\n    zipcodes = load_zipcodes(ZIP_XLSX_FILE)\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(zipcodes)} ZIP codes.\")\n\n    proxies = load_proxies(PROXY_LIST_FILE)\n    proxy_rotator = ProxyRotator(proxies)\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(proxies)} proxies.\")\n\n    zip_queue = queue.Queue()\n    result_queue = queue.Queue()\n    stop_event = threading.Event()\n\n    for zip_code in zipcodes:\n        zip_queue.put(zip_code)\n\n    # Start CSV writer thread\n    writer_thread = threading.Thread(\n        target=csv_writer,\n        args=(result_queue, OUTPUT_CSV_FILE, stop_event),\n        daemon=True\n    )\n    writer_thread.start()\n\n    # Start worker threads\n    threads = []\n    for _ in range(NUM_THREADS):\n        t = threading.Thread(\n            target=worker,\n            args=(zip_queue, proxy_rotator, result_queue),\n            daemon=True\n        )\n        t.start()\n        threads.append(t)\n\n    # Wait for all ZIP codes to be processed\n    zip_queue.join()\n    # Wait for all jobs to be written\n    result_queue.join()\n    # Signal writer to stop\n    stop_event.set()\n    writer_thread.join()\n    print(f\"Scraping complete. Results saved to {OUTPUT_CSV_FILE}\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()"

                        "import unittest\nimport tempfile\nimport os\nimport threading\nimport queue\nimport csv\nimport shutil\n\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\n\n# Import the functions/classes to test from the user's code.\n# To make this script runnable, we will redefine the relevant functions/classes inline.\n# (In practice, these would be imported from the module.)\n\n# ============================\n# Begin: Code Under Test\n# ============================\nimport requests\nfrom openpyxl import Workbook, load_workbook\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\ndef load_proxies(proxy_file):\n    proxies = []\n    if os.path.exists(proxy_file):\n        with open(proxy_file, \"r\") as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if line:\n                    proxies.append(line)\n    return proxies\n\nclass ProxyRotator:\n    def __init__(self, proxies):\n        self.proxies = proxies\n        self.lock = threading.Lock()\n        self.idx = 0\n\n    def get_proxy(self):\n        with self.lock:\n            if not self.proxies:\n                return None\n            proxy = self.proxies[self.idx % len(self.proxies)]\n            self.idx += 1\n            return {\n                \"http\": proxy,\n                \"https\": proxy\n            }\n\ndef load_zip_codes(xlsx_file, column_name):\n    wb = load_workbook(xlsx_file, read_only=True)\n    ws = wb.active\n    zip_codes = []\n    col_idx = None\n    for i, row in enumerate(ws.iter_rows(values_only=True)):\n        if i == 0:\n            # Find column index\n            for idx, val in enumerate(row):\n                if str(val).strip().upper() == column_name.upper():\n                    col_idx = idx\n                    break\n            if col_idx is None:\n                raise ValueError(f\"Column '{column_name}' not found in {xlsx_file}\")\n        else:\n            zip_code = row[col_idx]\n            if zip_code:\n                zip_codes.append(str(zip_code).strip())\n    return zip_codes\n\ndef scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip=20, search_query=\"software engineer\"):\n    jobs = []\n    INDEED_SEARCH_URL = \"https://www.indeed.com/jobs\"\n    HEADERS = {\n        \"User-Agent\": \"Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) \"\n                      \"AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like results_per_zip\n    }\n    proxy = proxy_rotator.get_proxy()\n    try:\n        resp = requests.get(INDEED_SEARCH_URL, headers=HEADERS, params=params, proxies=proxy, timeout=15)\n        if resp.status_code != 200:\n            return jobs\n        soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \"html.parser\")\n        job_cards = soup.find_all(\"div\", class_=\"job_seen_beacon\")\n        for card in job_cards:\n            title = card.find(\"h2\", class_=\"jobTitle\")\n            company = card.find(\"span\", class_=\"companyName\")\n            location = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"companyLocation\")\n            summary = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"job-snippet\")\n            job_link = card.find(\"a\", href=True)\n            job_url = \"https://www.indeed.com\" + job_link['href'] if job_link else \"\"\n            jobs.append({\n                \"zip_code\": zip_code,\n                \"title\": title.text.strip() if title else \"\",\n                \"company\": company.text.strip() if company else \"\",\n                \"location\": location.text.strip() if location else \"\",\n                \"summary\": summary.text.strip() if summary else \"\",\n                \"url\": job_url\n            })\n    except Exception as e:\n        pass\n    return jobs\n\ndef worker(zip_queue, proxy_rotator, csv_writer, csv_lock, results_per_zip, search_query):\n    import random\n    import time\n    while True:\n        try:\n            zip_code = zip_queue.get(timeout=3)\n        except queue.Empty:\n            break\n        jobs = zip_queue.task_done()\n        time.sleep(random.uniform(0.5, 1.5))  # Polite delay\n\n# ============================\n# End: Code Under Test\n# ============================\n\nclass                         "import unittest\nimport threading\nimport queue\nimport tempfile\nimport os\nimport csv\nfrom unittest import mock\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\nfrom openpyxl import Workbook\nimport sys\n\n# --- Import the code under test ---\n# For this test, we assume all functions/classes are in the same namespace.\n# If the code was in a module (e.g., indeed_scraper.py), you would use:\n# from indeed_scraper import *\n\n# To avoid running main() on import, we redefine main() as not to execute in test.\n\n# Copy the relevant functions/classes from the code to test here for direct testing.\n# (In a real scenario, you'd import them from the module.)\n\n# ============================\n# PROXY MANAGEMENT\n# ============================\ndef load_proxies(proxy_file):\n    proxies = []\n    if os.path.exists(proxy_file):\n        with open(proxy_file, \"r\") as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if line:\n                    proxies.append(line)\n    return proxies\n\nclass ProxyRotator:\n    def __init__(self, proxies):\n        self.proxies = proxies\n        self.lock = threading.Lock()\n        self.idx = 0\n\n    def get_proxy(self):\n        with self.lock:\n            if not self.proxies:\n                return None\n            proxy = self.proxies[self.idx % len(self.proxies)]\n            self.idx += 1\n            return {\n                \"http\": proxy,\n                \"https\": proxy\n            }\n\n# ============================\n# ZIP CODE LOADING\n# ============================\ndef load_zip_codes(xlsx_file, column_name):\n    from openpyxl import load_workbook\n    wb = load_workbook(xlsx_file, read_only=True)\n    ws = wb.active\n    zip_codes = []\n    col_idx = None\n    for i, row in enumerate(ws.iter_rows(values_only=True)):\n        if i == 0:\n            # Find column index\n            for idx, val in enumerate(row):\n                if str(val).strip().upper() == column_name.upper():\n                    col_idx = idx\n                    break\n            if col_idx is None:\n                raise ValueError(f\"Column '{column_name}' not found in {xlsx_file}\")\n        else:\n            zip_code = row[col_idx]\n            if zip_code:\n                zip_codes.append(str(zip_code).strip())\n    return zip_codes\n\n# ============================\n# SCRAPER LOGIC\n# ============================\ndef scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip=20, search_query=\"software engineer\"):\n    import requests\n    from bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n    INDEED_SEARCH_URL = \"https://www.indeed.com/jobs\"\n    HEADERS = {\n        \"User-Agent\": \"Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) \"\n                      \"AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) \"\n                      \"Chrome/122.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\"\n    }\n    jobs = []\n    params = {\n        \"q\": search_query,\n        \"l\": zip_code,\n        \"radius\": 15,\n        \"limit\": results_per_zip\n    }\n    proxy = proxy_rotator.get_proxy()\n    try:\n        resp = requests.get(INDEED_SEARCH_URL, headers=HEADERS, params=params, proxies=proxy, timeout=15)\n        if resp.status_code != 200:\n            print(f\"Failed to fetch jobs for ZIP {zip_code} (status {resp.status_code})\")\n            return jobs\n        soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \"html.parser\")\n        job_cards = soup.find_all(\"div\", class_=\"job_seen_beacon\")\n        for card in job_cards:\n            title = card.find(\"h2\", class_=\"jobTitle\")\n            company = card.find(\"span\", class_=\"companyName\")\n            location = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"companyLocation\")\n            summary = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"job-snippet\")\n            job_link = card.find(\"a\", href=True)\n            job_url = \"https://www.indeed.com\" + job_link['href'] if job_link else \"\"\n            jobs.append({\n                \"zip_code\": zip_code,\n                \"title\": title.text.strip() if title else \"\",\n                \"company\": company.text.strip() if company else \"\",\n                \"location\": location.text.strip() if location else \"\",\n                \"summary\": summary.text.strip() if summary else \"\",\n                \"url\": job_url\n            })\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error scraping ZIP {zip_code}: {e}\")\n    return jobs\n\n# ============================\n# MULTITHREADING WORKER\n# ============================\ndef worker(zip_queue, proxy_rotator, csv_writer, csv_lock, results_per_zip, search_query):\n    import time\n    import random\n    while True:\n        try:\n            zip_code = zip_queue.get(timeout=3)\n        except queue.Empty:\n            break\n        jobs = scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip, search_query)\n        with csv_lock:\n            for job in jobs:\n                csv_writer.writerow(job)\n        zip_queue.task_done()\n        time.sleep(random.uniform(0.5, 1.5))  # Polite delay\n\n# ============================\n# TEST SUITE\n# ============================\n\nclass TestIndeedScraper(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a temporary proxy file\n ProxyRotator instance\n        self.proxies = load_proxies(self.proxy_file.name)\n        self.proxy_rotator = ProxyRotator(self.proxies)\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n self.assertEqual(proxies[2][\"http\"], \"c\")\n        self.assertEqual(proxies[3][\"http\"], \"a\")\n        self.assertEqual(proxies[4][\"http\"], \"b\")\n\n    def test_proxy_rotator_empty(self):\n proxies\n        self.lock = threading.Lock()\n        self.idx = 0\n\n    def get_proxy(self):\n        \"\"\"Get the next proxy in a round-robin fashion.\"\"\"\n        with self.lock:\n            if not self.proxies:\n                return None\n            proxy = self.proxies[self.idx % len(self.proxies)]\n            self.idx += 1\n            return {\n                \"http\": proxy,\n                \"https\": proxy\n            }\n\n# ============================\n# ZIP CODE LOADING\n# ============================\ndef load_zip_codes(xlsx_file, column_name):\n    \"\"\"Load ZIP \"location\": location.text.strip() if location else \"\",\n                    \"summary\": summary.text.strip() if summary else \"\",\n                    \"url\": job_url\n                })\n            break  # Success, exit retry loop\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[{zip_code}] Error: {e} (attempt {attempt+1})\")\n            time.sleep(random.uniform(1, 2))\n    return \"\"\"\n    Worker thread: fetch jobs for ZIP codes from the queue and write to CSV.\n    \"\"\"\n    while True:\n        try:\n            zip_code = zip_queue.get(timeout=3)\n        except                         "import threading\nimport queue\nimport requests\nimport time\nimport random\nimport csv\nimport os\nfrom openpyxl import load_workbook\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# ============================\n# CONFIGURATION\n# ============================\nINDEED_SEARCH_URL = \"https://www.indeed.com/jobs\"\nHEADERS = {\n    \"User-Agent\": \"Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) \"\n                  \"AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) \"\n                  \"Chrome/122.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\"\n}\nNUM_THREADS = 32  # Increased for scalability\nPROXY_LIST_FILE = \"proxies.txt\"  # Each line: http://user:pass@ip:port or http://ip:port\nZIP_XLSX_FILE = \"zipcodes.xlsx\"  # Input file with ZIP codes\nZIP_COLUMN = \"ZIP\"  # Column name in XLSX file containing ZIP codes\nCSV_OUTPUT_FILE = \"indeed_jobs.csv\"\nSEARCH_QUERY = \"software engineer\"  # Example job query; change as needed\nRESULTS_PER_ZIP = 20  # Number of jobs to fetch per ZIP code\nMAX_RETRIES = 3  # Retry count per ZIP code\n\n# ============================\n# PROXY MANAGEMENT\n# ============================\ndef load_proxies(proxy_file):\n    proxies = []\n    if os.path.exists(proxy_file):\n        with open(proxy_file, \"r\") as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if line:\n                    proxies.append(line)\n    return proxies\n\nclass ProxyRotator:\n    def __init__(self, proxies):\n        self.proxies = proxies\n        self.lock = threading.Lock()\n        self.idx = 0\n\n    def get_proxy(self):\n        with self.lock:\n            if not self.proxies:\n                return None\n            proxy = self.proxies[self.idx % len(self.proxies)]\n            self.idx += 1\n            return {\n                \"http\": proxy,\n                \"https\": proxy\n            }\n\n# ============================\n# ZIP CODE LOADING\n# ============================\ndef load_zip_codes(xlsx_file, column_name):\n    wb = load_workbook(xlsx_file, read_only=True)\n    ws = wb.active\n    zip_codes = set()\n    col_idx = None\n    for i, row in enumerate(ws.iter_rows(values_only=True)):\n        if i == 0:\n            # Find column index\n            for idx, val in enumerate(row):\n                if str(val).strip().upper() == column_name.upper():\n                    col_idx = idx\n                    break\n            if col_idx is None:\n                raise ValueError(f\"Column '{column_name}' not found in {xlsx_file}\")\n        else:\n            zip_code = row[col_idx]\n            if zip_code:\n                zip_codes.add(str(zip_code).strip())\n    return list(zip_codes)\n\n# ============================\n# SCRAPER LOGIC\n# ============================\ndef scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip=20, search_query=\"software engineer\"):\n    jobs = []\n    params = {\n        \"q\": search_query,\n        \"l\": zip_code,\n        \"radius\": 15,\n        \"limit\": results_per_zip\n    }\n    for attempt in range(MAX_RETRIES):\n        proxy = proxy_rotator.get_proxy()\n        try:\n            resp = requests.get(INDEED_SEARCH_URL, headers=HEADERS, params=params, proxies=proxy, timeout=15)\n            if resp.status_code != 200:\n                print(f\"[{zip_code}] Status {resp.status_code}. Retrying ({attempt+1}/{MAX_RETRIES})...\")\n                time.sleep(random.uniform(1, 2))\n                continue\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \"html.parser\")\n            job_cards = soup.find_all(\"div\", class_=\"job_seen_beacon\")\n            for card in job_cards:\n                title = card.find(\"h2\", class_=\"jobTitle\")\n                company = card.find(\"span\", class_=\"companyName\")\n                location = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"companyLocation\")\n                summary = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"job-snippet\")\n                job_link = card.find(\"a\", href=True)\n                job_url = \"https://www.indeed.com\" + job_link['href'] if job_link else \"\"\n                jobs.append({\n                    \"zip_code\": zip_code,\n                    \"title\": title.text.strip() if title else \"\",\n                    \"company\": company.text.strip() if company else \"\",\n                    \"location\": location.text.strip() if location else \"\",\n                    \"summary\": summary.text.strip() if summary else \"\",\n                    \"url\": job_url\n                })\n            break  # Success, no need to retry\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[{zip_code}] Error: {e}. Retrying ({attempt+1}/{MAX_RETRIES})...\")\n            time.sleep(random.uniform(1, 2))\n    return jobs\n\n# ============================\n# MULTITHREADING WORKER\n# ============================\ndef worker(zip_queue, proxy_rotator, csv_writer, csv_lock, results_per_zip, search_query):\n    while True:\n        try:\n            zip_code = zip_queue.get(timeout=3)\n        except queue.Empty:\n            break\n        jobs = scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip, search_query)\n        if jobs:\n            with csv_lock:\n                for job in jobs:\n                    csv_writer.writerow(job)\n        zip_queue.task_done()\n        time.sleep(random.uniform(0.3, 0.9))  # Polite delay\n\n# ============================\n# MAIN PROGRAM\n# ============================\ndef main():\n    proxies = load_proxies(PROXY_LIST_FILE)\n    proxy_rotator = ProxyRotator(proxies)\n    zip_codes = load_zip_codes(ZIP_XLSX_FILE, ZIP_COLUMN)\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(zip_codes)} unique ZIP codes.\")\n\n    zip_queue = queue.Queue()\n    for zip_code in zip_codes:\n        zip_queue.put(zip_code)\n\n    fieldnames = [\"zip_code\", \"title\", \"company\", \"location\", \"summary\", \"url\"]\n    csv_lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    # Stream results to CSV\n    with open(CSV_OUTPUT_FILE, \"w\", newline='', encoding=\"utf-8\") as csvfile:\n        csv_writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        csv_writer.writeheader()\n\n        threads = []\n        for _ in range(NUM_THREADS):\n            t = threading.Thread(\n                target=worker,\n                args=(zip_queue, proxy_rotator, csv_writer, csv_lock, RESULTS_PER_ZIP, SEARCH_QUERY),\n                daemon=True\n            )\n            t.start()\n            threads.append(t)\n\n        # Wait for all ZIP codes to be processed\n        zip_queue.join()\n\n        # Wait for all threads to finish\n        for t in threads:\n            t.join()\n\n    print(f\"Scraping completed. Results saved to {CSV_OUTPUT_FILE}\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()"

open(proxy_file, \"r\") as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if line:\n                    proxies.append(line)\n    return proxies\n\nclass get_proxy(self):\n        \"\"\"Get the next proxy in a round-robin fashion.\"\"\"\n        with self.lock:\n            if not self.proxies:\n                return None\n            proxy = timeout=REQUEST_TIMEOUT)\n            if resp.status_code != 200:\n                print(f\"[{zip_code}] HTTP {resp.status_code} (attempt {attempt+1})\")\n                time.sleep(random.uniform(1, 2))\n                continue\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \"html.parser\")\n            job_cards = soup.find_all(\"div\", class_=\"job_seen_beacon\")\n            for card in job_cards:\n                title = card.find(\"h2\", class_=\"jobTitle\")\n                company = card.find(\"span\", class_=\"companyName\")\n                location = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"companyLocation\")\n                summary = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"job-snippet\")\n                job_link = card.find(\"a\", href=True)\n                job_url = \"https://www.indeed.com\" + job_link['href'] if job_link else \"\"\n                jobs.append({\n                    \"zip_code\": zip_code,\n                    \"title\": title.text.strip() if          \"AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) \"\n                  \"Chrome/122.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\"\n}\nMAX_RETRIES = 3\nREQUEST_TIMEOUT = 15\n\ndef load_proxies(proxy_file):\n    proxies = []\n    if os.path.exists(proxy_file):\n        with open(proxy_file, \"r\") as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if line:\n                    proxies.append(line)\n    return proxies\n\nclass ProxyRotator:\n    def __init__(self, proxies):\n        self.proxies = proxies\n        self.lock = threading.Lock()\n        self.idx = 0\n\n    def get_proxy(self):\n        with self.lock:\n            if not self.proxies:\n                return None\n            proxy = self.proxies[self.idx % len(self.proxies)]\n            self.idx += 1\n            return {\n                \"http\": proxy,\n                \"https\": proxy\n            }\n\ndef load_zip_codes(xlsx_file, column_name):\n    from openpyxl import load_workbook\n    wb = range(MAX_RETRIES):\n        proxy = proxy_rotator.get_proxy()\n        try:\n            resp = requests.get(INDEED_SEARCH_URL, headers=HEADERS, params=params, proxies=proxy, \"html.parser\")\n            job_cards = soup.find_all(\"div\", class_=\"job_seen_beacon\")\n            for card in job_cards:\n                title = card.find(\"h2\", class_=\"jobTitle\")\n class_=\"job-snippet\")\n                job_link = card.find(\"a\", href=True)\n                job_url = \"https://www.indeed.com\" + job_link['href'] if job_link else \"\"\n scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip, search_query)\n        with csv_lock:\n            for job in jobs:\n                csv_writer.writerow(job)\n scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip=20, search_query=\"software engineer\"):\n    \"\"\"\n    Scrape job postings from Indeed for a given ZIP code.\n    Uses proxy rotation and retries.\n    Returns a list of job dicts.\n    \"\"\"\n    from bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n    jobs = []\n    params = {\n        \"q\": search_query,\n        \"l\": zip_code,\n        \"radius\": 15,\n        \"limit\": results_per_zip\n    }\n    for attempt in range(MAX_RETRIES):\n        proxy = proxy_rotator.get_proxy()\n        try:\n            resp = requests.get(INDEED_SEARCH_URL,        continue\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \"html.parser\")\n            job_cards = soup.find_all(\"div\", class_=\"job_seen_beacon\")\n            for card in job_cards:\n                title = card.find(\"h2\", class_=\"jobTitle\")\n                company = card.find(\"span\", class_=\"companyName\")\n                location = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"companyLocation\")\n                summary = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"job-snippet\")\n                job_link = card.find(\"a\", href=True)\n                job_url = \"https://www.indeed.com\" + job_link['href'] if job_link else \"\"\n                jobs.append({\n                    \"zip_code\": zip_code,\n                    \"title\": title.text.strip() if title else \"\",\n                    \"company\": to CSV.\n    \"\"\"\n    while True:\n        try:\n            zip_code = zip_queue.get(timeout=0.1)\n        except queue.Empty:\n            break\n        jobs = scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip, search_query)\n        with csv_lock:\n            for job in jobs:\n                csv_writer.writerow(job)\n        zip_queue.task_done()\n        time.sleep(random.uniform(0, 0.01))\n\n# --- End code under test ---\n\nclass TestIndeedJobScraper(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Patch time.sleep to speed up tests\n ============================\ndef load_proxies(proxy_file):\n    \"\"\"Load proxies from a file, one per line.\"\"\"\n    proxies = []\n    if os.path.exists(proxy_file):\n        with open(proxy_file, \"r\") as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if line:\n                    proxies.append(line)\n    return proxies\n\nclass ProxyRotator:\n    \"\"\"Thread-safe proxy rotator.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, proxies):\n        self.proxies = proxies\n        self.lock = threading.Lock()\n        self.idx = 0\n\n    def get_proxy(self):\n        \"\"\"Get the next proxy in a round-robin fashion.\"\"\"\n        with self.lock:\n            if not self.proxies:\n                return None\n            proxy = self.proxies[self.idx % len(self.proxies)]\n            self.idx += 1\n            return {\n                \"http\": proxy,\n                \"https\": proxy\n            }\n\n# ============================\n# ZIP CODE LOADING\n# ============================\ndef load_zip_codes(xlsx_file, column_name):\n    \"\"\"Load ZIP codes from an XLSX file given a column name.\"\"\"\n  # Find column index\n            for idx, val in enumerate(row):\n                if str(val).strip().upper() == column_name.upper():\n                    col_idx = idx\n                    break\n            zip_codes.append(str(zip_code).strip())\n    return zip_codes\n\n# ============================\n# SCRAPER LOGIC\n# ============================\ndef scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip=20, search_query=\"software engineer\"):\n    \"\"\"\n    Scrape job postings from Indeed for a given ZIP code.\n    Uses proxy rotation and retries.\n    Returns a list of job dicts.\n    \"\"\"\n    jobs = []\n    params = {\n        \"q\": search_query,\n        \"l\": zip_code,\n        \"radius\": 15,\n        \"limit\": results_per_zip\n    }\n    for attempt in range(MAX_RETRIES):\n        proxy = proxy_rotator.get_proxy()\n        try:\n            resp = requests.get(INDEED_SEARCH_URL, headers=HEADERS, params=params, proxies=proxy, timeout=REQUEST_TIMEOUT)\n            if resp.status_code != 200:\n                print(f\"[{zip_code}] HTTP {resp.status_code} (attempt {attempt+1})\")\n                time.sleep(random.uniform(1, 2))\n                continue\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \"html.parser\")\n            job_cards = soup.find_all(\"div\", class_=\"job_seen_beacon\")\n            for card in job_cards:\n                title = card.find(\"h2\", class_=\"jobTitle\")\n                company = card.find(\"span\", class_=\"companyName\")\n                location = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"companyLocation\")\n                summary = card.find(\"div\", class_=\"job-snippet\")\n                job_link = card.find(\"a\", href=True)\n                job_url = \"https://www.indeed.com\" + job_link['href'] if job_link else \"\"\n                jobs.append({\n                    \"zip_code\": zip_code,\n                    \"title\": title.text.strip() if title else \"\",\n                    \"company\": company.text.strip() if company else \"\",\n                    \"location\": location.text.strip() if location else \"\",\n                    \"summary\": summary.text.strip().replace('\\n', ' ') if summary else \"\",\n                    \"url\": job_url\n                })\n            break  # Success, exit retry loop\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[{zip_code}] Error: {e} (attempt {attempt+1})\")\n            time.sleep(random.uniform(1, 2))\n    return jobs\n\n# ============================\n# MULTITHREADING WORKER\n# ============================\ndef worker(zip_queue, proxy_rotator, csv_writer, csv_lock, results_per_zip, search_query):\n    \"\"\"\n    Worker thread: fetch jobs for ZIP codes from the queue and write to CSV.\n    \"\"\"\n    while True:\n        try:\n            zip_code = zip_queue.get(timeout=3)\n        except queue.Empty:\n            break\n        jobs = scrape_indeed_jobs(zip_code, proxy_rotator, results_per_zip, search_query)\n        with csv_lock:\n            for job in jobs:\n                csv_writer.writerow(job)\n        zip_queue.task_done()\n        # Polite delay to avoid hammering Indeed, but short for scalability\n        time.sleep(random.uniform(0.2, 0.6))\n\n# ============================\n# MAIN PROGRAM\n# ============================\ndef main():\n    # Load proxies and ZIP codes\n    proxies = load_proxies(PROXY_LIST_FILE)\n    proxy_rotator = ProxyRotator(proxies)\n    zip_codes = zip_queue.put(zip_code)\n\n    fieldnames = [\"zip_code\", \"title\", \"company\", \"location\", \"summary\", \"url\"]\n    csv_lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    # Stream results to CSV (write as jobs    for _ in range(2):\n            t = threading.Thread(target=worker, args=(zip_queue, rotator, csv_writer, csv_lock, 1, \"engineer\"))\n            t.start()\n            threads.append(t)\n        zip_queue.join()\n        for t in threads:\n            t.join()\n        temp_csv.close()\n\n        with open(temp_csv.name, newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            reader = self.assertEqual(rows[0]['title'], 'ThreadTitle')\n        os.unlink(temp_csv.name)\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",
